if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '29d13228797bb0b9d922021bd02e3f7da5e78216') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '29d13228797bb0b9d922021bd02e3f7da5e78216') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'da49f46b9ca11f7318774b2ebc9c2c046f706b6a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '29d13228797bb0b9d922021bd02e3f7da5e78216') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') != '67b1bdf767aeb60443e30a12e0a3f88a191fd0f5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '67b1bdf767aeb60443e30a12e0a3f88a191fd0f5') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== 'd50e6c1506afb4d526462e97c28d390e89f07572') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps') !== '67b1bdf767aeb60443e30a12e0a3f88a191fd0f5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/translation/message_regenerate.phps');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') != 'fd23dc06e0be24a9965bc21c8250832b0c74ba0c') {

	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== 'fd23dc06e0be24a9965bc21c8250832b0c74ba0c') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}

		writefile_3();

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '3939b9fdbfeda41b600d40b2534764567b0a70a9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '3939b9fdbfeda41b600d40b2534764567b0a70a9') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '9bf308a1ee8c398c13e2fabd7c711df333cbd37f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '3939b9fdbfeda41b600d40b2534764567b0a70a9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != 'cc9688dc06f71e733a101c6b22431c94061bbb30') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'cc9688dc06f71e733a101c6b22431c94061bbb30') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '8c1b06c9fbac02e901d94eb7a2f151da2286889d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'cc9688dc06f71e733a101c6b22431c94061bbb30') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'fe754a671299af53938a76eb59b25fff24651a68') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'fe754a671299af53938a76eb59b25fff24651a68') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '611329c8c87ecdeb4a0bdfe153d97e90dc50f64b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'fe754a671299af53938a76eb59b25fff24651a68') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != '91342760d96ac31d4a59b4381ce7bb17a03ba3f0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '91342760d96ac31d4a59b4381ce7bb17a03ba3f0') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '901420084d3e009a29395b93f34b6b38f3d88679') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '91342760d96ac31d4a59b4381ce7bb17a03ba3f0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_8();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '8bdbbf40e3b4f1aa124ca90c847fd0c46d59449b') {

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');

} else {

				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '8bdbbf40e3b4f1aa124ca90c847fd0c46d59449b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 506\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 506') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
